(**
 1. Final object
 *)

B: bicat
x: B
Hx: is_bifinal x
is_bifinal x


B: bicat
x: B
Hx: is_bifinal x
is_bifinal x

  
B: bicat
x: B
Hx: is_bifinal x
bifinal_1cell_property x
B: bicat
x: B
Hx: is_bifinal x
∏ Y : op2_bicat B, bifinal_2cell_property x Y
B: bicat
x: B
Hx: is_bifinal x
∏ Y : op2_bicat B, bifinal_eq_property x Y

  
B: bicat
x: B
Hx: is_bifinal x
bifinal_1cell_property x
 exact (λ y, is_bifinal_1cell_property Hx y).
  
B: bicat
x: B
Hx: is_bifinal x
∏ Y : op2_bicat B, bifinal_2cell_property x Y
 exact (λ y f g, is_bifinal_2cell_property Hx y g f).
  
B: bicat
x: B
Hx: is_bifinal x
∏ Y : op2_bicat B, bifinal_eq_property x Y
 exact (λ y f g α β, is_bifinal_eq_property Hx y g f α β).
Defined.

(**
 2. Products

Section ProductOp2.
  Context {B : bicat}
          {a x y : B}
          (p₁ : a --> x)
          (p₂ : a --> y)
          (cone := make_binprod_cone a p₁ p₂)
          (ump : has_binprod_ump cone).

  Definition op2_binprod_cone
    : @binprod_cone (op2_bicat B) x y
    := make_binprod_cone a p₁ p₂.

  
B: bicat
a, x, y: B
p₁: B ⟦ a, x ⟧
p₂: B ⟦ a, y ⟧
cone:= make_binprod_cone a p₁ p₂: binprod_cone x y
ump: has_binprod_ump cone
q: binprod_cone x y
binprod_1cell q op2_binprod_cone

  
B: bicat
a, x, y: B
p₁: B ⟦ a, x ⟧
p₂: B ⟦ a, y ⟧
cone:= make_binprod_cone a p₁ p₂: binprod_cone x y
ump: has_binprod_ump cone
q: binprod_cone x y
binprod_1cell q op2_binprod_cone

a, x, y: B

ump: has_binprod_ump cone
q: binprod_cone x y
k₁:= binprod_cone_pr1 q: op2_bicat B ⟦ q, x ⟧
binprod_1cell q op2_binprod_cone

k₂:= binprod_cone_pr2 q: op2_bicat B ⟦ q, y ⟧
binprod_1cell q op2_binprod_cone

a, x, y: B

q: op2_bicat B
φ, ψ: op2_bicat B ⟦ q, op2_binprod_cone ⟧
α: φ · binprod_cone_pr1 op2_binprod_cone ==>
ψ · binprod_cone_pr1 op2_binprod_cone
β: φ · binprod_cone_pr2 op2_binprod_cone ==>
ψ · binprod_cone_pr2 op2_binprod_cone
∃! γ : φ ==> ψ,
γ ▹ binprod_cone_pr1 op2_binprod_cone = α
× γ ▹ binprod_cone_pr2 op2_binprod_cone = β

ψ · binprod_cone_pr1 op2_binprod_cone
β: φ · binprod_cone_pr2 op2_binprod_cone ==>
ψ · binprod_cone_pr2 op2_binprod_cone
isaprop
  (∑ γ : φ ==> ψ,
   γ ▹ binprod_cone_pr1 op2_binprod_cone = α
   × γ ▹ binprod_cone_pr2 op2_binprod_cone = β)

 abstract
        (use invproofirrelevance ;
         intros φ₁ φ₂ ;
         use subtypePath ; [ intro ; apply isapropdirprod ; apply cellset_property | ] ;
         exact (binprod_ump_2cell_unique_alt
                  ump
                  _ _
                  (pr12 φ₁ @ !(pr12 φ₂))
                  (pr22 φ₁ @ !(pr22 φ₂)))).

(**
 3. Mirroring pullbacks
 *)
Definition mirror_cone
           {B : bicat}
           {x y z : B}
           {f : x --> z}
           {g : y --> z}
           (p : pb_cone f g)
  : pb_cone g f
  := make_pb_cone
       p
       (pb_cone_pr2 p) (pb_cone_pr1 p)
       (inv_of_invertible_2cell (pb_cone_cell p)).

Section Mirroring.
  Context {B : bicat}
          {pb x y z : B}
          {f : x --> z}
          {g : y --> z}
          {p₁ : pb --> x}
          {p₂ : pb --> y}
          {γ : invertible_2cell (p₁ · f) (p₂ · g)}
          (cone := make_pb_cone pb p₁ p₂ γ)
          (pb_sqr : has_pb_ump cone).

  
B: bicat
pb, x, y, z: B
f: B ⟦ x, z ⟧
g: B ⟦ y, z ⟧
p₁: B ⟦ pb, x ⟧
p₂: B ⟦ pb, y ⟧
γ: invertible_2cell (p₁ · f) (p₂ · g)
cone:= make_pb_cone pb p₁ p₂ γ: pb_cone f g
pb_sqr: has_pb_ump cone
has_pb_ump (mirror_cone cone)

  
B: bicat
pb, x, y, z: B
f: B ⟦ x, z ⟧
g: B ⟦ y, z ⟧
p₁: B ⟦ pb, x ⟧
p₂: B ⟦ pb, y ⟧
γ: invertible_2cell (p₁ · f) (p₂ · g)
cone:= make_pb_cone pb p₁ p₂ γ: pb_cone f g
pb_sqr: has_pb_ump cone
has_pb_ump (mirror_cone cone)

    
B: bicat
pb, x, y, z: B
f: B ⟦ x, z ⟧
g: B ⟦ y, z ⟧
p₁: B ⟦ pb, x ⟧
p₂: B ⟦ pb, y ⟧
γ: invertible_2cell (p₁ · f) (p₂ · g)
cone:= make_pb_cone pb p₁ p₂ γ: pb_cone f g
pb_sqr: has_pb_ump cone
pb_ump_1 (mirror_cone cone)
B: bicat
pb, x, y, z: B
f: B ⟦ x, z ⟧
g: B ⟦ y, z ⟧
p₁: B ⟦ pb, x ⟧
p₂: B ⟦ pb, y ⟧
γ: invertible_2cell (p₁ · f) (p₂ · g)
cone:= make_pb_cone pb p₁ p₂ γ: pb_cone f g
pb_sqr: has_pb_ump cone
pb_ump_2 (mirror_cone cone)

    
B: bicat
pb, x, y, z: B
f: B ⟦ x, z ⟧
g: B ⟦ y, z ⟧
p₁: B ⟦ pb, x ⟧
p₂: B ⟦ pb, y ⟧
γ: invertible_2cell (p₁ · f) (p₂ · g)
cone:= make_pb_cone pb p₁ p₂ γ: pb_cone f g
pb_sqr: has_pb_ump cone
pb_ump_1 (mirror_cone cone)
 
B: bicat

f: B ⟦ x, z ⟧

B: bicat
pb, x, y, z: B
f: B ⟦ x, z ⟧
g: B ⟦ y, z ⟧
p₁: B ⟦ pb, x ⟧
p₂: B ⟦ pb, y ⟧
γ: invertible_2cell (p₁ · f) (p₂ · g)
cone:= make_pb_cone pb p₁ p₂ γ: pb_cone f g
pb_sqr: has_pb_ump cone
q: pb_cone g f
pb_ump_mor pb_sqr (mirror_cone q)
◃ pb_cone_cell (mirror_cone cone) =
(((lassociator (pb_ump_mor pb_sqr (mirror_cone q))
     (pb_cone_pr1 (mirror_cone cone)) g
   • (pb_ump_mor_pr2 pb_sqr (mirror_cone q) ▹ g))
  • pb_cone_cell q)
 • ((pb_ump_mor_pr1 pb_sqr (mirror_cone q)) ^-1 ▹ f))
• rassociator (pb_ump_mor pb_sqr (mirror_cone q))
    (pb_cone_pr2 (mirror_cone cone)) f
 abstract
          (pose (r := pb_ump_mor_cell pb_sqr (mirror_cone q)) ;
           cbn in r ;
           cbn ;
           rewrite !vassocl ;
           use vcomp_move_L_pM ; [ is_iso | ] ; cbn ;
           use vcomp_move_R_Mp ; [ is_iso | ] ; cbn ;
           rewrite !vassocl ;
           use vcomp_move_L_pM ; [ is_iso ; apply property_from_invertible_2cell | ] ;
           cbn ;
           use vcomp_move_L_pM ; [ is_iso ; apply property_from_invertible_2cell | ] ;
           cbn ;
           do 2 (use vcomp_move_L_pM ; [ is_iso | ] ; cbn) ;
           rewrite !vassocl in r ;
           exact (!r)).

B: bicat
pb, x, y, z: B
f: B ⟦ x, z ⟧
g: B ⟦ y, z ⟧
p₁: B ⟦ pb, x ⟧
p₂: B ⟦ pb, y ⟧
γ: invertible_2cell (p₁ · f) (p₂ · g)
cone:= make_pb_cone pb p₁ p₂ γ: pb_cone f g
pb_sqr: has_pb_ump cone
w: B
φ, ψ: B ⟦ w, mirror_cone cone ⟧
α: φ · pb_cone_pr1 (mirror_cone cone) ==>
ψ · pb_cone_pr1 (mirror_cone cone)
β: φ · pb_cone_pr2 (mirror_cone cone) ==>
ψ · pb_cone_pr2 (mirror_cone cone)
q: (((φ ◃ pb_cone_cell (mirror_cone cone))
  • lassociator φ (pb_cone_pr2 (mirror_cone cone))
      f) • (β ▹ f))
• rassociator ψ (pb_cone_pr2 (mirror_cone cone)) f =
((lassociator φ (pb_cone_pr1 (mirror_cone cone)) g
  • (α ▹ g))
 • rassociator ψ (pb_cone_pr1 (mirror_cone cone))
     g) • (ψ ◃ pb_cone_cell (mirror_cone cone))
∃! γ : φ ==> ψ,
γ ▹ pb_cone_pr1 (mirror_cone cone) = α
× γ ▹ pb_cone_pr2 (mirror_cone cone) = β

 • rassociator ψ (pb_cone_pr1 (mirror_cone cone))
     g) • (ψ ◃ pb_cone_cell (mirror_cone cone))
(λ _ : pb_ump_cell pb_sqr φ ψ β α
         (mirror_has_pb_ump_subproof1 w φ ψ α β q)
       ▹ pb_cone_pr1 (mirror_cone cone) = α,
 pb_ump_cell pb_sqr φ ψ β α
   (mirror_has_pb_ump_subproof1 w φ ψ α β q)
 ▹ pb_cone_pr2 (mirror_cone cone) = β)
  (pb_ump_cell_pr2 pb_sqr φ ψ β α
     (mirror_has_pb_ump_subproof1 w φ ψ α β q))
 exact (pb_ump_cell_pr1 pb_sqr φ ψ β α _).
  Defined.
End Mirroring.

         pose (pb_ump_mor_cell H (from_op2_pb_cone q)) as p ; cbn in p ;
         use vcomp_move_L_pM ; [ is_iso | ] ;

         cbn ;
         rewrite !vassocl ;
         use vcomp_move_L_pM ; [ is_iso ; apply property_from_invertible_2cell | ] ;
         use vcomp_move_L_pM ;
         [ apply from_op2_is_invertible_2cell ;
           apply property_from_invertible_2cell

         cbn ;
         use vcomp_move_L_pM ; [ is_iso ; apply property_from_invertible_2cell | ] ;
         use vcomp_move_L_pM ; [ is_iso | ] ;
         cbn ;
         refine (_ @ !p) ;
         rewrite !vassocl ;
         apply idpath).
  Defined.

w: op2_bicat B
φ, ψ: op2_bicat B ⟦ w, to_op2_pb_cone γ ⟧
α: φ · pb_cone_pr1 (to_op2_pb_cone γ) ==>
ψ · pb_cone_pr1 (to_op2_pb_cone γ)
β: φ · pb_cone_pr2 (to_op2_pb_cone γ) ==>

• ((β ▹ g) • (rassociator φ p₂ g • (φ ◃ γ ^-1))) =
(ψ ◃ γ ^-1)
• (lassociator ψ p₁ f
   • ((α ▹ f) • rassociator φ p₁ f))
∃! γ0 : φ ==> ψ,
γ0 ▹ pb_cone_pr1 (to_op2_pb_cone γ) = α
× γ0 ▹ pb_cone_pr2 (to_op2_pb_cone γ) = β

• ((β ▹ g) • (rassociator φ p₂ g • (φ ◃ γ ^-1))) =
(ψ ◃ γ ^-1)
• (lassociator ψ p₁ f
   • ((α ▹ f) • rassociator φ p₁ f))
isaprop
  (∑ γ0 : φ ==> ψ,
   γ0 ▹ pb_cone_pr1 (to_op2_pb_cone γ) = α
   × γ0 ▹ pb_cone_pr2 (to_op2_pb_cone γ) = β)
 abstract
        (use invproofirrelevance ;
         intros ζ₁ ζ₂ ;
         use subtypePath ; [ intro ; apply isapropdirprod ; apply cellset_property | ] ;
         use (pb_ump_eq H _ _ α β _ _ _ (pr12 ζ₁) (pr22 ζ₁) (pr12 ζ₂) (pr22 ζ₂)) ;
         cbn ; cbn in p ;
         rewrite !vassocl ;
         use vcomp_move_R_pM ; [ is_iso ; apply property_from_invertible_2cell | ] ;
         cbn ;
         rewrite !vassocr ;
         use vcomp_move_L_Mp ; [ is_iso ; apply property_from_invertible_2cell | ] ;
         cbn ;
         rewrite !vassocl ;
         exact p).

p₁: B ⟦ pb, x ⟧
p₂: B ⟦ pb, y ⟧
γ: invertible_2cell (p₁ · f) (p₂ · g)
cone:= make_pb_cone pb p₁ p₂ γ: pb_cone f g
H: has_pb_ump cone
w: op2_bicat B
φ, ψ: op2_bicat B ⟦ w, to_op2_pb_cone γ ⟧
α: φ · pb_cone_pr1 (to_op2_pb_cone γ) ==>
ψ · pb_cone_pr1 (to_op2_pb_cone γ)
β: φ · pb_cone_pr2 (to_op2_pb_cone γ) ==>
ψ · pb_cone_pr2 (to_op2_pb_cone γ)
p: lassociator ψ p₂ g
• ((β ▹ g) • (rassociator φ p₂ g • (φ ◃ γ ^-1))) =
(ψ ◃ γ ^-1)
• (lassociator ψ p₁ f
   • ((α ▹ f) • rassociator φ p₁ f))
∑ γ0 : φ ==> ψ,
γ0 ▹ pb_cone_pr1 (to_op2_pb_cone γ) = α
× γ0 ▹ pb_cone_pr2 (to_op2_pb_cone γ) = β

  • lassociator φ (comma_cone_pr2 op2_comma_cone)
      f) • (β ▹ f))

((lassociator φ (comma_cone_pr1 op2_comma_cone) g
  • (α ▹ g))
 • rassociator ψ (comma_cone_pr1 op2_comma_cone) g)
• (ψ ◃ comma_cone_cell op2_comma_cone)
(λ _ : comma_ump_cell comma_sqr ψ φ β α
         (op2_comma_has_comma_ump_2_subproof0 q φ ψ α
            β p) ▹ comma_cone_pr1 op2_comma_cone = α,
 comma_ump_cell comma_sqr ψ φ β α
   (op2_comma_has_comma_ump_2_subproof0 q φ ψ α β p)
 ▹ comma_cone_pr2 op2_comma_cone = β)
  (op2_comma_has_comma_ump_2_subproof1 q φ ψ α β p)
 abstract (apply (comma_ump_cell_pr1 comma_sqr)).
  Defined.

Defined.

            • lassociator g₁
                (mor_of_em_comnd_cone m e)
                (endo_of_mnd m)))))

   (mor_of_em_comnd_cone m e)

     ▹ mor_of_em_comnd_cone m e)

              (mor_of_em_comnd_cone m e)
              (endo_of_mnd m)))))

Definition op2_bicat_has_em
           {B : bicat}
           (HB : has_em_comnd B)
  : bicat_has_em (op2_bicat B)
  := λ m,
     let e := HB m
     in em_comnd_cone_to_op2_em_cone (pr1 e) ,, op2_bicat_has_em_ump (pr2 e).
